| 1:12:44| the proposed hillside and ridgetop protection plan.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4364)|
| 1:12:47| The coalition consists of member neighborhoods, Colonial Village, Island Home Park,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4367)|
| 1:12:52| Lake Forest, Old Sevier, South Haven, Southside Riverfront, and South Woodlawn,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4372)|
| 1:12:58| as well as the Downtown South Business Association.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4378)|
| 1:13:01| We voted unanimously to request your support for this plan.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4381)|
| 1:13:05| We want to thank the Joint City-County Task Force and MPC staff for working so diligently| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4385)|
| 1:13:10| to create a plan that preserves the natural beauty of East Tennessee| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4390)|
| 1:13:14| and reduces erosion, flooding, and harm to water quality,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4394)|
| 1:13:18| while allowing for responsible development.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4398)|
| 1:13:21| One part of the plan we were particularly happy to see are the incentives for developers,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4401)|
| 1:13:26| such as the density bonus provisions for those who put the steeper portion of their property| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4406)|
| 1:13:30| into conservative easement.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4410)|
| 1:13:33| Providing incentives for quality development is an excellent policy.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4413)|
| 1:13:37| Extensive community input has gone into this plan over a long period of time.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4417)|
| 1:13:42| Its development involved multiple meetings of the task force and its subcommittees,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4422)|
| 1:13:47| nine community meetings and surveys.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4427)|
| 1:13:50| The draft plan was then presented in two public meetings and discussed at three MPC meetings,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4430)|
| 1:13:55| a joint MPC-City Council workshop and other MPC workshops.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4435)|
| 1:14:00| We would ask you to note that this plan is not land use regulation.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4440)|
| 1:14:05| It's a policy document which will guide the development and revision of some land use regulations.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4445)|
| 1:14:11| Those will all come before this body for review and approval.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4451)|
| 1:14:14| But this plan itself is policy, not regulation.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4454)|
| 1:14:19| The task force and MPC staff sought to achieve a balance between conservation| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4459)|
| 1:14:24| and development on hillsides and ridges, with policies that would foster hillside development| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4464)|
| 1:14:29| while protecting both environmental resources and property rights.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4469)|
| 1:14:33| We believe they have achieved that balance, and we ask that you please vote to approve this plan as presented.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom110228part2?start=4473)|
